SAMPLE     (82-PB-208,ENR=0.99) The targets were made by          C2700  4    6 
           evaporating lead metal enriched to 99% in 208Pb from   C2700  4    7 
           a tungsten boat onto glass slides that were            C2700  4    8

REACTION   (82-PB-208(P,INL)82-PB-208,PAR,DA)                     C2700  7    3 
FACILITY   (VDG,1USATEX) The University of Texas Van de Graaff    C2700  7    4 
           accelerators in three-stage operation.                 C2700  7    5 
SAMPLE     (82-PB-208,ENR=0.99) The targets were made by          C2700  7    6 
           evaporating lead metal enriched to 99% in 208Pb from   C2700  7    7 
           a tungsten boat onto glass slides that were            C2700  7    8 
           previously coated with a very thin film of a           C2700  7    9 
           detergent. It turned out to be 0.71 mg/cm2. This       C2700  7   10 
           corresponds to an energy loss of about 7.5 keV for     C2700  7   11 
           16.0-MeV protons as they penetrate through the target. C2700  7   12

SAMPLE     (82-PB-208,ENR=0.99) The targets were made by          C2700  8    6 
           evaporating lead metal enriched to 99% in 208Pb from   C2700  8    7 
           a tungsten boat onto glass slides that were            C2700  8    8 
           previously coated with a very thin film of a           C2700  8    9 
           detergent. It turned out to be 0.71 mg/cm2. This       C2700  8   10 
           corresponds to an energy loss of about 7.5 keV for     C2700  8   11 
           16.0-MeV protons as they penetrate through the target. C2700  8   12

           accelerators in three-stage operation.                 C2700  9    5 
SAMPLE     (82-PB-208,ENR=0.99) The targets were made by          C2700  9    6 
           evaporating lead metal enriched to 99% in 208Pb from   C2700  9    7 
           a tungsten boat onto glass slides that were            C2700  9    8 
           previously coated with a very thin film of a           C2700  9    9 
           detergent. It turned out to be 0.71 mg/cm2. This       C2700  9   10 
           corresponds to an energy loss of about 7.5 keV for     C2700  9   11 
           16.0-MeV protons as they penetrate through the target. C2700  9   12 
DETECTOR   (SILI) Four 3-mm-thick ORTEC SiLi detectors were used  C2700  9   13 
           in this experiment. They were placed at 90, 12, 150,   C2700  9   14 
           and 170 degrees to the incident beam and cooled to     C2700  9   15 
           approximately dry-ice temperature.                     C2700  9   16

SAMPLE     (82-PB-208,ENR=0.99) The targets were made by          C2700 10    6 
           evaporating lead metal enriched to 99% in 208Pb from   C2700 10    7 
           a tungsten boat onto glass slides that were            C2700 10    8 
           previously coated with a very thin film of a           C2700 10    9 
           detergent. It turned out to be 0.71 mg/cm2. This       C2700 10   10 
           corresponds to an energy loss of about 7.5 keV for     C2700 10   11 
           16.0-MeV protons as they penetrate through the target. C2700 10   12
